msg:The lobby is on the 64th floor, and we checked in when we arrived at the store at 11 o'clock. To get to the guest room, we need to change to the elevator, and the road is a bit devious. The room is arranged on the 67th floor, and outside the window is the Guomao CBD with a small waist and big pants. The floor-to-ceiling windows have a nice view, but the glass outside the window is a little dirty, probably because of the rain yesterday.
The room was spacious and the socket complex next to the desk was also a UPS. I just like the large private bathroom, which is separated from wet and dry, and the shower room can be seated. The TV is hidden in the washing mirror. There is even a separate dressing room outside the door, but the girls complain that the lighting is yellowish.
From 6:00 to 8:00 in the evening, the 80th Floor Yunku Lounge has Happy Time, a drink before dinner, and a buffet of hot and cold snacks. It faces west and focuses on sunset views.
Breakfast is on the 79th floor, facing the rising sun, you can see the Forbidden City. Breakfast is self-service or a la carte. Although there are not many varieties, the quality is not bad.
The gymnasium and swimming pool on the 78th floor have a large area and complete facilities. The 25-meter infinity pool has clear water quality and comfortable water temperature, and bottled water can be seen everywhere.
The downstairs of the hotel is connected to the China World Mall. It is convenient to go shopping, eat and take the subway.
Generally speaking, the service staff I met were enthusiastic, giving people a friendly and comfortable feeling.
However, the hotel's WiFi is not strong, and it is not easy to take a taxi.

There are two independent rooms in the toilet, namely the toilet room (with smart toilet cover) and the shower room. Outside the two independent rooms are Two washbasins, the mirror on the washbasin is equipped with a smart TV, and there is a bathtub opposite the washbasin. There is also a dressing room (table) outside the bathroom, and two large wardrobes. There is a dressing table in the powder room. There are two boxes of tissues and three trash cans in the toilet and powder room respectively. The details of the toilet are particularly well thought out!
Third, the infinity pool and gym are great! The swimming pool can see the invincible scenery outside, as well as the massage pool, etc. The gym is also equipped with various fitness equipment such as treadmills, and there are enough water and towels.
Fourth, it is super convenient to go and eat. Downstairs is the China World Mall, and the fourth floor is the corridor. You can walk there and stroll around in the north, central and south areas. It took us a day and a half to finally figure it out. Here, you can enjoy food, clothing, housing, and travel without leaving home. Unless you need to come out for nucleic acid production, you don‚Äôt have to go out at all for three days inside.


A little more regret.
The executive lounge trea**ent and beds are a bit regrettable. In addition, the 64th floor is the front desk for check-in and check-out, especially from 12:00 to 2:00, check-out and check-in peak, here is slightly congested, the key is that there is no sign, it is all manual, where to check in and check out, Put a sign at the front desk!
Regret 1, the size of the bedroom is not small, that is, the bed is not big, two single beds of 1 meter wide, if it is a double bed, it is also 2 meters wide. Now many hotels have single beds, 1.2 meters or even 1.35 meters, such a good room, the details of the bathroom are thought a lot, that is, the bed is a little narrower, I really hope the bed is wider, the high-end hotel is 1 meter wide The bed is very rare now!
The second regret is also the biggest regret. Executive lounge, much lower than expected. We really came for the executive lounge. The trea**ent of the executive lounge in other hotels is a quiet environment and exquisite snacks. The 64th floor is where check-in is. Drinks and snacks are all here. Catching up with the peak check-in period, it is particularly congested and a little messy. Happy hour on the 80th floor in the evening, catching up with three cold dishes (all salads), three hot dishes (all fried food), drinks are good, even here is a mess, the food table is too small, and there are many people in line , Can you put more food counters? So, the executive lounge doesn't feel good. After staying for three days and two nights, I only enjoyed the happy hour once, the food on the 64th floor, and seeing so many people, I lost my appetite. The lounge on the 64th floor has few dim sum choices and a lot of people. Compared with the executive lounge trea**ent of other hotels, there is less food and more people. I went there once during the afternoon tea time, and it felt good. There were not too many people and it was not noisy. The snacks to choose from were relatively rich.
I would like to make a small suggestion, whether it is possible to improve the trea**ent of the executive lounge, even if you add a little more money, put the executive lounge on the 79th or 80th floor. There is no need to put food on the 64th floor, a little drink is enough. Otherwise, the 64th floor is too congested.

I have stayed in many five-star hotels, and the experience of China World Hotel is very different this time. China World Hotel is on the upper floors, the entire hotel is above the 64th floor, and the front desk is on the 64th floor. When you enter the building, take the elevator up to the 64th floor, which is like a plane or high-speed rail, and you can reach the 64th floor in less than a minute. After various registrations at the front desk, the staff will guide you to the room.

It should be noted that although the scenery is very good on the upper floors, the scenery is different in different directions. Generally speaking, the main thing to stay here is to look at the big pants and the Chinese Zun, so you have to propose to live in the east room before you check in, so if there is one, they will arrange the east room. I didn't tell the front desk when I went, they arranged a west facing location on the 73rd floor. After entering the room, I thought about it or wanted to communicate with the front desk, and even wanted to make up the difference to go to a better room. After communication, I changed a room on the 72nd floor of Chaodong at the same price, which satisfied the idea of watching the night view of CCTV and China Zun. (There are many sceneries in the photo)

The interior is more than 50 square meters, bedroom, cloakroom, dressing table, shower room, bathtub, vanity, toilet, drink bar, desk, beauty lying, coffee table, TV, and the fantasy of entering the door to change shoes, all facilities are readily available. Toiletries are all made by L‚ÄôOccitane and are of high quality. The bathtub is also equipped with bath salts, so you can take a comfortable bath.

It should be noted that, as required, toothbrushes, toothpaste, combs, and razors are no longer supplied with the room. If needed, call the service depar**ent and they will be delivered. Generally speaking, the front desk will ask you if you need it before you check in and arrange for someone to deliver it to your room. This is good, everyone is responsible for environmental protection! The bed is super large and comfortable, I don't know where I went to sleep when I fell asleep in the middle of the night. I was still thinking about why I have grown up in sleeping postures and I finally know the answer. It turns out that the bed is not big enough, hahahaha!

There are two kinds of pillows to choose from, feather pillows and high-grade foam pillows. I like the harder foam pillows. The feather pillows are soft and flat, and feel comfortable to the touch. It's too low to fall asleep. The bathtub is super big, and the anti-slip mats are carefully prepared. Put two bags of sea salt and soak beautifully for half an hour. After getting up, put on your bathrobe and you can lie in front of the floor-to-ceiling windows and enjoy the high-rise scenery.

After entering the room, the waiter kindly brought fruit and tableware. There were also various drinks in the mini bar next to it, such as Coke, Sprite, apple juice, orange juice, Tsingtao beer, mineral water, tea, coffee, and coffee machines. , What do you want to drink? Very considerate! This time I didn't eat at the hotel, and I didn't have the habit of eating breakfast. I had to leave before noon, so I didn't order breakfast. The front desk said that if you need to have a meal, you can go upstairs to pay the bill and check out together when you check out, which is very convenient.

When checking out, the front desk presented a set of exquisite coasters, a total of six, they are the coasters of their top bar, very exquisite. In addition, downstairs is the China World Mall, where you can find all kinds of food and famous shops. You can go directly to the mall downstairs. In addition to the shops, the mall has all kinds of detailed settings and many novelty gadgets.

All in all, it was a great experience. It was the first time I lived in the International Trade CBD in Beijing for so many years. It was a very satisfying trip to enjoy the stay.
